Tolerant of partial failure —\n5\tone surface failing doesn't block others.\n6\t\n7\tSurfaces:\n8\t  INTERNAL → MCClient (task updates, approvals, board memory)\n9\t  PUBLIC → GHClient (branches, PRs)\n10\t  CHANNEL → IRCClient (IRC messages)\n11\t  NOTIFY → NtfyClient (human notifications)\n12\t  PLANE → PlaneClient (Plane issue updates — optional)\n13\t  META → logging, metrics\n14\t\n15\t> \"smart tools, chains that will trigger multiple things for one call\n16\t> or one event and that will keep listening to all side and keep in sync\"\n17\t\"\"\"\n18\t\n19\tfrom __future__ import annotations\n20\t\n21\timport logging\n22\tfrom typing import Optional\n23\t\n24\tfrom fleet.core.event_chain import ChainResult, Event, EventChain, EventSurface\n25\t\n26\tlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n27\t\n28\t\n29\tclass ChainRunner:\n30\t    \"\"\"Executes event chains across surfaces.\n31\t\n32\t    Usage::\n33\t\n34\t        runner = ChainRunner(mc=mc_client, irc=irc_client, gh=gh_client,\n35\t                             plane=plane_client, ntfy=ntfy_client)\n36\t        result = await runner.run(chain)\n37\t    \"\"\"\n38\t\n39\t    def __init__(\n40\t        self,\n41\t        mc=None,\n42\t        irc=None,\n43\t        gh=None,\n44\t        plane=None,\n45\t        ntfy=None,\n46\t        board_id: str = \"\",\n47\t        plane_workspace: str = \"fleet\",\n48\t    ) -> None:\n49\t        self._mc = mc\n50\t        self._irc = irc\n51\t        self._gh = gh\n52\t        self._plane = plane\n53\t        self._ntfy = ntfy\n54\t        self._board_id = board_id\n55\t        self._plane_ws = plane_workspace\n56\t\n57\t    async def run(self, chain: EventChain) -> ChainResult:\n58\t        \"\"\"Execute all events in the chain. Tolerant of partial failure.\"\"\"\n59\t        result = ChainResult(\n60\t            operation=chain.operation,\n61\t            total_events=len(chain.events),\n62\t        )\n63\t\n64\t        for event in chain.events:\n65\t            try:\n66\t                await self._execute_event(event)\n67\t                event.executed = True\n68\t                result.executed += 1\n69\t            except Exception as e:\n70\t                event.error = str(e)\n71\t                event.executed = True\n72\t                if event.required:\n73\t                    result.failed += 1\n74\t                    result.errors.append(\n75\t                        f\"[{event.surface.value}] {event.action}: {e}\"\n76\t                    )\n77\t                else:\n78\t                    # Non-required failures logged but don't fail the chain\n79\t                    logger.warning(\n80\t                        \"Non-required event failed: [%s] %s: %s\",\n81\t                        event.surface.value, event.action, e,\n82\t                    )\n83\t\n84\t        return result\n85\t\n86\t    async def _execute_event(self, event: Event) -> None:\n87\t        \"\"\"Dispatch an EventSurface.CHANNEL: self._handle_channel,\n92\t            EventSurface.NOTIFY: self._handle_notify,\n93\t            EventSurface.META: self._handle_meta,\n94\t        }\n95\t\n96\t        # PLANE handlers.get(event.surface)\n101\t        if handler:\n102\t            event.result = await handler(event)\n103\t        else:\n104\t            logger.warning(\"No handler for surface: %s\", event.surface)\n105\t\n106\t    # ─── Surface Handlers ──────────────────────────────────────────────\n107\t\n108\t    async def _handle_internal(self, event: Event) -> dict:\n109\t        \"\"\"Handle INTERNAL events — MC task updates, approvals, board memory.\"\"\"\n110\t        if not self._mc:\n111\t            raise RuntimeError(\"MCClient not available\")\n112\t\n113\t        action = event.action\n114\t        params = event.params\n115\t\n116\t        if action == \"update_task_status\":\n117\t            task_id = params.get(\"task_id\", \"\")\n118\t            status = params.get(\"status\", \"\")\n119\t            if task_id and status:\n120\t                await self._mc.update_task(\n121\t                    self._board_id, task_id, status=status,\n122\t                )\n123\t                return {\"updated\": task_id, \"status\": status}\n124\t\n125\t        elif action == \"create_approval\":\n126\t            task_id = params.get(\"task_id\", content:\n140\t                await self._mc.post_memory(\n141\t                    self._board_id,\n142\t                    content=content,\n143\t                    tags=tags,\n144\t                )\n145\t                return {\"memory_posted\": True}\n146\t\n147\t        elif action == \"post_comment\":\n148\t            task_id = params.get(\"task_id\", \"\")\n149\t            comment =             )\n154\t                return {\"comment_posted\": task_id}\n155\t\n156\t        return {\"action\": action, \"status\": \"no_handler\"}\n157\t\n158\t    async def _handle_public(self, The orchestrator reads this file\n5\teach cycle to detect outages without needing the agent to be alive.\n6\t\n7\tThis is a file-based approach because:\n8\t1. pauses entirely until the service recovers.\n12\t\"\"\"\n13\t\n14\tfrom __future__ import annotations\n15\t\n16\tfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\n17\tfrom datetime import datetime, call.\"\"\"\n46\t        s = self._services.get(service)\n47\t        if s:\n48\t            s.healthy = True\n49\t            s.consecutive_failures = 0\n50\t            s.last_success_at = now = datetime.now()\n56\t        s = self._services.get(service)\n57\t        if not s:\n58\t            return\n59\t\n60\t        s.consecutive_failures += 1\n61\t        s.last_failure_at = 480)\n66\t        s.backoff_until = now + timedelta(seconds=backoff_seconds)\n67\t\n68\t        if s.consecutive_failures >= 3:\n69\t            s.healthy = False\n70\t\n71\t    def datetime.now()\n74\t        s = self._services.get(service)\n75\t        if not s:\n76\t            return True\n77\t\n78\t        if s.backoff_until and now < s.backoff_until:\n79\t            return Last: {mc.last_error}\"\n93\t\n94\t        if mc and mc.backoff_until and now < mc.backoff_until:\n95\t            remaining = (mc.backoff_until - now).total_seconds()\n96\t            return False, f\"MC API backoff: {remaining:.0f}s remaining\"\n97\t\n98\t        return True, \"\"\n99\t\n100\t    def get_alerts(self) -> list[str]:\n101\t        \"\"\"Get alert messages for unhealthy services.\"\"\"\n102\t        alerts = []\n103\t        for s in self._services.values():\n104\t            if not s.healthy:\n105\t                alerts.append(\n106\t                    f\"{s.name}: DOWN ({s.consecutive_failures} failures, \"\n107\t                    f\"last: {s.last_error[:50]})\"\n108\t                )\n109\t        return alerts\n110\t\n111\t    def format_status(self) -> str:\n112\t        \"\"\"Format service health for display.\"\"\"\n113\t        lines = []\n114\t        for s in self._services.values():\n115\t            icon = \"✅\" if s.healthy else \"❌\"\n116\t            lines.append(f\"{icon} {s.name}: {'healthy' if s.healthy else f'DOWN ({s.consecutive_failures} failures)'}\")\n117\t        return \" | \".join(lines)"}]},"uuid":"bd0fe793-6c6f-47ca-a40d-e51f5d927349","timestamp":"2026-03-29T21:50:44.542Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"34b9b5f3-a080-48d6-aab5-c0e47fd004e0","userType":"external","entrypoint":"claude-vscode","cwd":"/home/jfortin/devops-expert-local-ai","sessionId":"08087abb-77a7-48cc-a71e-d33c7116faa7","version":"2.1.86","gitBranch":"main","slug":"polished-hatching-hellman"}

This is acceptable for optional surfaces but makes debugging hard\n\n- **Line 360-382 (fleet_commit)**: Direct git calls via `ctx.gh._run()` — uses private method\n  - Should use public API if available\n\n- **Line 385-658 (fleet_task_complete)**: MONOLITHIC — does 7 things at once\n  - No event chain, all inline\n  - If any step fails, user gets error\n  - Should use `ChainRunner` with partial failure tolerance\n\n- **Line 456-470**: Test execution before PR (quality gate)\n  - Not part of spec but good pattern\n  - Not configurable; routing logic embedded in tools\n\n**Fire-and-Forget Issues:**\n\n- **Line 315-322**: IRC notifications wrapped in try/except — if notification fails, tool succeeds anyway\n  - This is intentional (optional surface) but prevents observability\n\n- **Line 626-633, 692**: Same pattern for all IRC calls\n\n- **Line 804, 857**: Ntfy publication failures silently pass\n\n**Missing Functionality:**\n\n- No call to `ChainRunner` or `build_task_complete_chain()` in `fleet_task_complete()`\n- No event emission when tasks transition between statuses\n- No use of `NotificationRouter` for deduplication in tools\n- Plane tools (14-20) don't emit events; they make direct API calls only\n\n**Integration Gaps:**\n\n- **Should use**: `build_task_complete_chain()` + `ChainRunner` to handle multi-surface notifications\n- **Currently does**: Manual API calls with hardcoded channel routing\n- **Cost**: If one surface fails (e.g., ntfy down), no recovery; user must re-run\n- **Observability**: Hard to track which surfaces succeeded/failed per operation\n\n---\n\n### CLI & ORCHESTRATION\n\n#### 14. `/home/jfortin/openclaw-fleet/fleet/cli/orchestrator.py`\n- **Status**: COMPLETE\n- **Events**: INDIVIDUAL_CALLS (orchestrates task transitions, no event emission)\n- **Anti-patterns**:\n  - Event infrastructure exists but is not used\n   - MCP tools use direct point-to-point API calls instead of chains\n   - Orchestrator doesn't use event chains for task transitions\n   - **Impact**: No atomic multi-surface operations; if one surface fails, partial state corruption\n\n2. **Missing Event Emission**\n   - Task status transitions don't emit events\n   - Task creation doesn't emit events\n   - Approvals don't emit events\n   - **Impact**: Hard to trace causal chains; difficult debugging\n\n3. **No Observability**\n   - IRC notifications are fire-and-forget\n   - Ntfy notifications are optional and silently dropped\n   - No way to know if all surfaces succeeded for an operation\n   - **Impact**: Silent failures when ntfy is down\n\n4. **Hardcoded Routing**\n   - Channel names hardcoded (#fleet, #reviews, #alerts)\n   - IRC template selection embedded in tools\n   - No routing configuration\n   - **Impact**: Channel routing can't be changed without code changes\n\n5. **Missing Error Handling**\n   - `error_reporter.report_error()` is never called\n   - Agents don't report errors to orchestrator\n   - Orchestrator can't detect agent failures except via timeout\n   - **Impact**: Silent agent failures; orchestrator unaware of problems\n\n6. **Unused Detectors**\n   - `OutageDetector` created but `should_run_cycle()` not called\n   - `remote_watcher` imported but never used\n   - **Impact**: Outage detection capability disabled\n\n### Anti-Pattern Instances:\n\n| File | Line(s) | Anti-Pattern | Severity |\n|------|---------|--------------|----------|\n| chain_runner.py | 96-98 | Defensive hasattr check | Low |\n| chain_runner.py | 111, 161, 181 | RuntimeError for missing clients | Medium |\n| notification_router.py | 141 | Magic strings for severity | Low |\n| routing.py | 105-127 | Hardcoded keyword scoring | Medium |\n| remote_watcher.py | 120-127 | Fragile regex intent detection | Medium |\n| error_reporter.py | 84 | Silent failures | Low |\n| mcp/tools.py | 315-322, 626-633, etc | Except: pass on IRC/ntfy | Medium |\n| mcp/tools.py | 360-382 | Private method usage (_run) | Low |\n| mcp/tools.py | 385-658 | Monolithic fleet_task_complete | High |\n| mcp/tools.py | Throughout | Hardcoded channels | Medium |\n| orchestrator.py | 431-443 | Early return on rate limit | Medium |\n| orchestrator.py | 687 | OutageDetector created but unused | High |\n| daemon.py | 136-150 | Non-event-driven health check | Medium |\n| sync.py | 71-88, 114-139 | Auto-transitions without events | Medium |\n\n---\n\n## RECOMMENDATIONS\n\n### Priority 1: CRITICAL (Fix immediately)\n\n1. **Connect MCP tools to event bus**\n   - Replace `fleet_task_complete()` monolith with `build_task_complete_chain()` + `ChainRunner`\n   - Use event emission for all multi-surface operations\n   - Guarantees atomic all-or-partial success\n\n2. **Activate OutageDetector**\n   - Call `should_run_cycle()` in orchestrator before each cycle\n   - Pause dispatch if services are unhealthy\n   - Log to error_reporter for visibility\n\n3. **Implement error reporting in agents**\n   - Add try/except wrapper in each MCP tool\n   - Call `error_reporter.report_error()` on failures\n   - Orchestrator can detect agent failures\n\n### Priority 2: HIGH (Fix within sprint)\n\n4. **Make remote_watcher production-ready**\n   - Import and use in sync.py or orchestrator\n   - Detect human PR comments and task updates\n   - Emit events for orchestrator to act on\n\n5. **Remove fire-and-forget notification pattern**\n   - Use `NotificationRouter` for all IRC/ntfy calls\n   - Track which surfaces succeeded\n   - Retry failed surfaces\n\n6. **Externalize hardcoded routing**\n   - Move channel names to config (fleet.yaml)\n   - Use `NotificationRouter.route_channel()` from all tools\n   - Allow multi-destination routing (e.g., both #fleet and #alerts)\n\n### Priority 3: MEDIUM (Refactor)\n\n7. **Decompose fleet_task_complete()**\n   - Split into: build chain → run chain → handle results\n   - Each step is testable\n   - Errors are observable\n\n8. **Make error_reporter active**\n   - Agents wrap tool calls and report errors\n   - Orchestrator reads error log each cycle\n   - Backoff logic triggers on repeated failures\n\n9. **Add event streaming**\n   - The system works but uses bypass plumbing (direct MCP→API calls) instead of the designed arterial system (event chains). This creates:\n\n- No atomic multi-surface operations\n- Silent failures on optional surfaces\n- Hard debugging when things go wrong\n- Dead code in remote_watcher and outage_detector\n- Missed observability opportunities\n\n**Recommendation**: Make event buses the primary path for all multi-surface operations within the next 2 sprints.
